              <div class="post-content">
               <h1 class="post-title" itemprop="name">
                <a href="https://www.sea7htravel.com/2018/07/Tourism.in.lankaran.azerbaijan.html" itemprop="url" title="السياحة في لنكران أذربيجان ">
                 السياحة في لنكران أذربيجان
                </a>
               </h1>
               <div itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="https://schema.org/Person">
                <meta content="https://plus.google.com/108020332453507578101" itemprop="url"/>
                <meta content="najeeb kassab" itemprop="name"/>
               </div>
               <div class="post-entry">
                <p itemprop="description">
                 السياحة في لنكران أذربيجان    وهي مدينة رائعة الجمال تقع جنوب شرق أذربيجان ويبلغ عدد سكانها حوالي 196 ألف نسمة ويحدها بحر القزوين في الجنو...
                </p>
               </div>
               <div class="post-more">

                </a>

 ( function( $ ) {
     "use strict";
     $( document ).ready( function() {
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Is to disable the preloader when the page finish load!
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         setTimeout( function() {
           $( "#loader" ).css( "display", "none" );
         }, 400 );
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Add parent class to navigation parents
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $( ".mainmenu .menu ul > li > ul" ).parent().addClass( "parent" );
         $( ".mainmenu .menu ul > li.parent" ).hover( function() {
             $( this ).children( ".mainmenu .menu ul > li > ul" ).slideDown( 300 );
         }, function() {
             $( this ).children( ".mainmenu .menu ul > li > ul" ).slideUp( 300 );
         } );
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Header Mobile Menu
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $( ".mobile-tigger" ).on( "click", function() {
             $( ".mobile-nav" ).slideToggle( 200 );
             $( ".mobile-wrap" ).toggleClass( "open" );
         } );
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Header Search Toggle
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $( ".search-tigger,.search-close" ).on( "click", function() {
             $( ".search-form" ).toggleClass( "open" );
         } );
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Sticky Header
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $( ".mainmenu" ).stickMe();
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // This is function to activate the Sticky Sidebar Plugin
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         jQuery( ".sidebar" ).theiaStickySidebar( {
             // Settings
             additionalMarginTop: 60
         } );
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Activate Match Height Plugin
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $( ".blog-posts .row" ).each( function() {
             $( this ).children( ".post" ).matchHeight();
         } );
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Lazy Load Activated
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $( "img.lazy" ).unveil( 200, function() {
             $( this ).load( function() {
                 this.style.opacity = 1;
             } );
         } );
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Scroll To Top
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $( window ).scroll( function() {
             if ( $( this ).scrollTop() > 100 ) {
                 $( ".totop" ).fadeIn();
             } else {
                 $( ".totop" ).fadeOut();
             }
         } );
         $( ".totop" ).on('click', function() {
             $( "html, body" ).animate( {
                 scrollTop: 0
             }, 600 );
             return false;
         } );
     } );
 } )( jQuery );

         });
         for (var i = 0; s >= i; i++) a += "</ul>", t += "</ul>", 0 != i && (a +=
             "</li>", t += "</li>");
         $(".mainmenu .PageList .nav").html(t);
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Blocks Feeds Script
         // ------------------------------------------------------
     	function blockfeeds(parent, count, label, style) {
 
           // Image Optimizations
           function opImages(img, size, w, h) {
               return img.replace(size, 'w' + w + '-h' + h)
           }
 
           // FEED URL & No Thumb & Months Name Variable
           var furl = "",
               startIndex = Math.floor((Math.random() * count) + 1),
               noThumb = "//3.bp.blogspot.com/-DB4ttXv4Iz8/WJ83ZTz4U3I/AAAAAAAABIU/UKJ-pggs-mwbwjXw-d6jHWCAUVz-M7kPgCK4B/w400-h320/no_image.jpg";
 
           // JSON FEED
           if (label !== undefined) {
               if (label.match('recent')) {
                   furl = '/feeds/posts/summary?alt=json-in-script&max-results=' + count;
               }else if (label.match("random")) {
                   furl = '/feeds/posts/summary?alt=json-in-script&orderby=updated&start-index=' + startIndex + '&max-results=' + count;
               }else if (label.match('discussed')) {
                   furl = '/feeds/posts/summary?alt=json-in-script&max-results=9999';
               }else if (!(label.match('random')) || !(label.match('recent')) || !(label.match('discussed')) ) {
                   furl = '/feeds/posts/summary/-/' + label + '?alt=json-in-script&max-results=' + count;
               }
           }
 
           // AJAX FUNCTION
           if (furl.length > 0) {
               $.ajax({
                   type: 'GET',
                   url: furl,
                   cache: false,
                   dataType: 'jsonp',
                   beforeSend: function(){
                       parent.html('<div class="loading"><div class="spinner"></div></div>');
                   },
                   complete: function(){
                       $('.loader-icon').hide();
                   },
                   success: function(data) {
                       // First Tag of Block Content
                       var htmlcode= '';
                       switch(style){
                           case 'featured':
                             htmlcode += '<div class="row-gallery">';
                             break;
                           case 'trending':
                             htmlcode += '<div class="slider">';
                             break;
                           case 'feeds':
                             htmlcode += '<ul class="recent-posts">';
                             break;
                           case 'related':
                             htmlcode += '<div class="content row-medium">';
                             break;
                           default:
                             htmlcode += '<ul>';
                             break;
                       }
 
                       var feedcode = '',
                           link = '',
                           json = data.feed.entry;
 
                       // Sortby Most Commented
                           if (label.match('discussed')) {
                              var dataLength = count;
                               // Sortby Most Commented
                               function compare(a,b) {
                                 return  (b.thr$total.$t- a.thr$total.$t)
                               }
                               data.feed.entry.sort(compare);
                           } else {
                              var dataLength = json.length;
                           }
 
                       // The Loop
                       for (var i=0; i<dataLength; i++) {
 
                           // Get link from an array
                           for (var j = 0; j < json[i].link.length; j++) {
                               if (json[i].link[j].rel == "alternate") {
                                   link = json[i].link[j].href;
                                   break;
                               }
                           }
 
                           // Get Entry Feeds
                           var title = json[i].title.$t,
                               author = json[i].author[0].name.$t,
                               content = json[i].summary.$t,
                               $content = $('<div>').html(content),
                               shortSummary = $content.text().substr(0, 110) + '...',
                               longSummary = $content.text().substr(0, 210) + '...';
 
                           // Get One Category
                           if ('category' in json[i]) {
                             if (json[i].category[0].term !== undefined) {
                                 var tag = json[i].category[0].term;
                             }
                           } else {
                             var tag = 'Uncategorized';
                           }
 
                           // Get Thumbnail Image as globale
                           //if (content.indexOf("<img") !== -1 || content.indexOf("youtube.com/embed") !== -1) {
                               if(json[i].media$thumbnail != undefined) {
                                   var src = json[i].media$thumbnail.url;
                               }
                           //}
 
                           // Optmize Images
                           if (src !== undefined) {
                               if (src.match("default.jpg")) {
                                   var $src = src.replace(
                                       "/default.jpg",
                                       "/hqdefault.jpg");
                               }
                               switch(style){
                                   case 'featured':
                                           if (src.match("s72")) {
                                               if (i === 0) {
                                                 var $src = opImages(src, "s72", 1328, 1004);
                                               } else {
                                                 var $src = opImages(src, "s72", 948, 500);
                                               }
                                           }
                                     break;
                                   case 'trending':
                                           if (src.match("s72")) {
                                              var $src = opImages(src, "s72", 317, 238);
                                           }
                                     break;
                                   case 'related':
                                           if (src.match("s72")) {
                                              var $src = opImages(src, "s72", 303, 170);
                                           }
                                     break;
                                   default:
                                           if (src.match("s72")) {
                                              var $src = opImages(src, "s72", 90, 70);
                                           }
                                     break;
                               }
                           }
 
                           // Variables for easy add!
                           var thumb = '<div class="post-thumb"><a href="' + link + '"><img class="lazy" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NGenkBIMa34/WEyH4J3cWXI/AAAAAAAAA6g/VjT9teL76qsCGgYZWU7LfBC_PxxRWF4swCK4B/s1/placeholder.png" data-src="'
                           + $src + '" alt="' + title +'"/></a></div>',
                               postTitle = '<a href="' + link + '">' + title + '</a>',
                               metaTag = '<div class="post-category"><a href="/search/label/' + tag + '?max-results=11">' + tag + '</a></div>',
                               shortSum = '<p class="post-entry">' + shortSummary + '</p>',
                               longSum = '<p class="post-entry">' + longSummary + '</p>';
 
 
                           // Block Content
                           switch(style){
                               case 'featured':
                                   if( i === 0 ){
                                       htmlcode += '<div class="first col-md-8 col-sm-12"><div class="post has-caption" style="background-image: url(' +
                                                   $src + ');"><div class="post-content"><h2 class="post-title">' +
                                                   postTitle + '</h2></div></div></div>';
                                   } else {
                                       htmlcode += '<div class="col-md-4 col-sm-4"><div class="post has-caption" style="background-image: url(' +
                                                   $src + ');"><div class="post-content"><h4 class="post-title">' +
                                                   postTitle + '</h4></div></div></div>';
                                   }
                                 break;
                               case 'trending':
                                   htmlcode += '<div class="item"><div class="post">' +
                                                   thumb + '<div class="post-content"><h4 class="post-title">' +
                                                   postTitle + '</h4></div></div></div>';
                                 break;
                               case 'related':
                                   htmlcode += '<div class="col-md-4 col-sm-4 col-xs-4"><article class="post">' +
                                                   thumb + '<div class="post-content"><h6 class="post-title">' +
                                                   postTitle + '</h6></div></article></div>';
                                 break;
                               default:
                                   htmlcode += '<span class="error-loading">حدث خطأ أثناء تحميل الإضافة، جرب تغيير الإعدادات حسب التوثيق!</span>';
                                 break;
                           }
 
                       }
 
                       feedcode += '</ul>';
                       htmlcode += feedcode;
 
                       switch(style){
                           case 'featured':
                             htmlcode += '</div>';
                             break;
                           case 'trending':
                             htmlcode += '</div><div id="trendNav" class="slider-nav"></div>';
                             break;
                           case 'related':
                             htmlcode += '</div>';
                             break;
                           default:
                             htmlcode += '</ul>';
                             break;
                       }
 
                       // Print The Resultsa s HTML
                         parent.html(htmlcode);
 
                       // ------------------------------------------------------
                       // Trending Places Slider Activated
                       // ------------------------------------------------------
                       var trendingSlider = $( ".trending-places .slider" );
                       trendingSlider.owlCarousel( {
                           items: 3,
                           loop: true,
                           rtl: true,
                           autoplay: true,
                           smartSpeed: 500,
                           autoplayTimeout: 3000,
                           autoplayHoverPause: true,
                           nav: true,
                           navContainer: '#trendNav',
                           navText: [ '', '' ],
                           dots: true,
                           dotsEach: true,
                           margin: 10,
                           responsiveClass: true,
                           responsive: {
                               0: {
                                   items: 1
                               },
                               480: {
                                   items: 2
                               },
                               768: {
                                   items: 3
                               },
                               992: {
                                   items: 3
                               }
                           }
                       } );
                       // ------------------------------------------------------
                       // Unveil Plugin Activated
                       // ------------------------------------------------------
                           $("img.lazy").unveil(10, function() {
                             $(this).load(function() {
                               this.style.opacity = 1;
                             });
                           });
 
                   },
                   error: function() {
                       parent.html('حدث خطأ أثناء تحميل الخلاصات! ربما هنالك مقال غير مصنف! يرجى التأكد من أن مشاركتك تحتوي على تصنيف واحد على الأقل.');
                   }
               });
           }
     	};
 
   		// Activate Ajax Feeds
         $(".featured-posts .widget-content,.trending-places .widget-content,.sidebar .HTML .widget-content,.footer-col .HTML .widget-content,.related").each(function() {
             var $this = $(this),
                 sp = $this.text().split("/");
 
                 if(!isNaN(sp[0])){
                   var count = sp[0],
                       style = sp[1],
                       label = sp[2];
 
                   blockfeeds($this, count, label, style);
                 }
         });
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Optimize Images
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $(".popular-posts img").attr('src', function(i, src) {
             return src.replace('w72-h72-p-k-no-nu', 'w90-h80-c-k-no');

             );

                     '<div class="contact-form"><form name="contact-form"><p class="contact-form-name"><label for="name">إسمك الكامل :</label><input class="contact-form-name" id="ContactForm1_contact-form-name" name="name" size="30" value="" type="text" /></p><p class="contact-form-email"><label for="email"> بريدك الإلكتروني : <span class="required" >(حقل مطلوب*)</span></label><input class="contact-form-email" id="ContactForm1_contact-form-email" name="email" size="30" value="" type="text" /></p><p class="contact-form-message"><label for="message">رسالتك : <span class="required">(حقل مطلوب*)</span></label><textarea class="contact-form-email-message"  id="ContactForm1_contact-form-email-message" name="email-message" cols="25" rows="5"></textarea></p><p class="contact-form-submit"><input class="contact-form-button contact-form-button-submit" id="ContactForm1_contact-form-submit" value="إرسال الرسالة" type="button" /></p><div class="contact-notifications"><p class="contact-form-error-message" id="ContactForm1_contact-form-error-message"></p><p class="contact-form-success-message" id="ContactForm1_contact-form-success-message"></p></div></form></div>'
                 );
         });
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         // Post Advertisement
         // ------------------------------------------------------
         $('.post-body *').replaceText(/(\(post_ads\))/g, '<div class="inner-ads" id="hassen"></div>');
         $('.inner-ads').append($('#HTML5').html());
         $('#HTML5').remove();

             $('.loadMorePosts').hide();
             $.ajax({
               url: olderLink,
               success: function(html){
                 var res = $(html).find('.blog-posts .row');
                 res.children(".status-msg-wrap").remove();
                 $('.blog-posts .row').append(res.html());
                 olderLink = $(html).find('.blog-pager-older-link').attr("href");
                 if (olderLink)
                   $('.loadMorePosts').show();
 				else
                   $('#postsloaded').show();
 
                   // ------------------------------------------------------
                   // Unveil Plugin Activated
                   // ------------------------------------------------------
                     $("img.lazy").unveil(10, function() {
                       $(this).load(function() {
                         this.style.opacity = 1;
                       });
                     });
                   // ------------------------------------------------------
                   // Post Excrept
                   // ------------------------------------------------------
                     $('.long-snippet').each(function(){
                       var txt = $(this).text();
                       $(this).text(txt.substr(0, 150).replace(/[?,!\.-:;]*$/, '...'));
                     });
                   // ------------------------------------------------------
                   // Activate Match Height Plugin
                   // ------------------------------------------------------
                   $( ".blog-posts .row" ).each( function() {
                       $( this ).children( ".post" ).matchHeight();
                   } );
               },
               beforeSend: function() {
                 $('#moreloader').show();
               },
               complete: function() {
                 $('#moreloader').hide();
               }
             });
           })
